int main(int argc, char *argv[])
{
  if (argc != 3)
  {
    fprintf(stderr, "Usage: %s <source> <destination>\n", argv[0]);
    exit(EXIT_FAILURE);
  }

  int source = open(argv[1], O_RDONLY);
  if (source == -1)
  {
    perror("Source file open error");
    exit(EXIT_FAILURE);
  }

  int destination = open(argv[2], O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_TRUNC, 0666);
  if (destination == -1)
  {
    perror("Destination file open error");
    exit(EXIT_FAILURE);
  }

  copy_file(source, destination);

  close(source);
  close(destination);

  return 0;
}

  to = open("file2.txt", O_WRONLY | O_CREAT, S_IRUSR | S_IWUSR);

  close(to);

void copy_file(int from, int to)
{
  char buffer[1024];

  int n;
  while ((n
                'VARIABLE'
                Complete the 'VARIABLE' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'VARIABLE'. 
                
Time taken: 3.1217739582061768 seconds
Received response: != 0)
  {
    n = read(from, buffer, sizeof(buffer));
    if (n < 0)
    {
      perror("read");
      return;
    }

    int offset = 0;
    while (n > 0)
    {
      int written = write(to, buffer + offset, n);
      if (written < 0)
      {
        perror("write");
        return;
      }

      n -= written;
      offset += written;
    }
  }
}

int main(int argc, char *argv[])
{
  if (argc < 3)
  {
    fprintf(stderr, "Usage: %s <from> <to>\n", argv[0]);
    return 1;
  }

  int from = open(argv[1], O_RDONLY);
  if (from < 0)
  {
    perror("open");
    return 1;
  }

  int to = open(argv[2], O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_TRUNC, 0664);
  if (to < 0)
  {
    perror("open");
    return 1;
  }

  copy_file(from, to);

  close(from);
  close(to);

  return 0;
}

    fprintf(stderr, "Usage: %s <from-file> <to-file>\n", argv[0]);
    return 1;

    return 1;

  copy_file(from, to);

  close(to);
